A glimpse #behindthescenes  in our Editorial department. https://t.co/Q8jLgtowGz #7 What's at stake behind the scientific claim? Who has something to gain? Or something to lose? #questionstoask #dayoffacts #6 Could there be another explanation for a claim? How much data was collected? #questionstoask #dayoffacts #2 Who is making the claim? Is the source respected? Peer-reviewed? Who paid for the research? #questionstoask #dayoffacts #1 What exactly is the claim? Read carefully.
